\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00945}00945 \textcolor{comment}{  \(\backslash\)c Neumann\_bc flag to \(\backslash\)c true and specifying}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00948}00948 \textcolor{comment}{The implementation is straightforward and actually}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00949}00949 \textcolor{comment}{presents an instructive exercise. [Suggestion: Rather than }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00950}00950 \textcolor{comment}{incorporating the additional functionality directly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00951}00951 \textcolor{comment}{into the existing Poisson elements, use inheritance to create a new}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00952}00952 \textcolor{comment}{class, \(\backslash\)c PoissonEquationsWithFluxBC, say, which contains}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00953}00953 \textcolor{comment}{the additional data and provides the necessary access functions. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00954}00954 \textcolor{comment}{The derived class must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00955}00955 \textcolor{comment}{overload \(\backslash\)c get\_residuals(...) with a function that initially calls \(\backslash\)c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00956}00956 \textcolor{comment}{PoissonEquations:get\_residuals(...) and then adds the }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00957}00957 \textcolor{comment}{contribution from the line integrals]. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00958}00958 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00959}00959 \textcolor{comment}{Unfortunately, the implementation suggested above has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00960}00960 \textcolor{comment}{several serious disadvantages}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00961}00961 \textcolor{comment}{-\/\# The test of \(\backslash\)c Neumann\_bc[i] must be performed }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00962}00962 \textcolor{comment}{   in every element, even though only a relatively small number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00963}00963 \textcolor{comment}{   elements are likely to be located on the domain boundaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00964}00964 \textcolor{comment}{-\/\# The code that implements the computation of the integrals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00965}00965 \textcolor{comment}{   along the four possible element edges is very similar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00966}00966 \textcolor{comment}{   (the main difference being which local coordinate is held}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00967}00967 \textcolor{comment}{   constant along the appropriate element edge, and which }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00968}00968 \textcolor{comment}{   local nodes make a contribution to the element residual vector)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00969}00969 \textcolor{comment}{   but this similarly is not exploited.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00970}00970 \textcolor{comment}{-\/\# Finally, and most significantly, many steps in the above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00971}00971 \textcolor{comment}{   procedure, such as the identification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00972}00972 \textcolor{comment}{   of the nodes that are located on specific element edges, are }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00973}00973 \textcolor{comment}{   completely generic and will also occur in the application of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00974}00974 \textcolor{comment}{   Neumann-\/type boundary conditions in other equations (see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00975}00975 \textcolor{comment}{   section ***). Incorporating the procedure directly into }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00976}00976 \textcolor{comment}{   the Poisson elements makes it impossible to "{}reuse"{} the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00977}00977 \textcolor{comment}{   relevant algorithms elsewhere.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00978}00978 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00979}00979 \textcolor{comment}{Our implementation employs a slightly different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00980}00980 \textcolor{comment}{approach: rather than incorporating the assembly of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00981}00981 \textcolor{comment}{boundary integral into the Poisson element itself, we treat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00982}00982 \textcolor{comment}{the boundary integral over the element's face as a distinct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00983}00983 \textcolor{comment}{lower-\/dimensional \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement. We separate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00984}00984 \textcolor{comment}{the specification of the element geometry from the implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00985}00985 \textcolor{comment}{of the specific boundary conditions, and use templating and inheritance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00986}00986 \textcolor{comment}{to create Neumann-\/type elements for entire families }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00987}00987 \textcolor{comment}{of elements. Here will discuss the \(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElement class,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00988}00988 \textcolor{comment}{a class of \(\backslash\)c FiniteElements that impose flux boundary conditions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00989}00989 \textcolor{comment}{on the "{}faces"{} of associated "{}bulk"{} Poisson elements. The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l00990}00990 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElement class is}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01002}01002 \textcolor{comment}{Our implementation involves two new classes:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01032}01032 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)e e.g. the four-\/node quad element \(\backslash\)c QPoissonElement<2,2>, }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01033}01033 \textcolor{comment}{the nine-\/node quad element  \(\backslash\)c QPoissonElement<2,3>, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01034}01034 \textcolor{comment}{Here is the constructor for the \(\backslash\)c FluxPoissonProblem class:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01035}01035 \textcolor{comment}{\(\backslash\)code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01036}01036 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01037}01037 \textcolor{comment}{//========================================================================}\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01038}01038 \textcolor{comment}{/// \(\backslash\)short Constructor for Poisson problem with prescribed flux boundary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01039}01039 \textcolor{comment}{/// conditions. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01040}01040 \textcolor{comment}{}//========================================================================}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01041}01041 template<class ELEMENT>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01042}01042 FluxPoissonProblem<ELEMENT>::FluxPoissonProblem()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01043}01043 \{ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01044}01044  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01045}01045  // Build and assign mesh (3 x 4 elements in unit square)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01046}01046  Problem::mesh\_pt()=new SimpleRectangularQuadMesh<ELEMENT>(3,4,1.0,1.0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01047}01047 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01048}01048 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01049}01049 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01050}01050 As always, we start by creating a mesh, specifying the type of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01051}01051 "{}bulk"{} element as the template argument in the mesh constructor. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01052}01052 When the mesh generation process is complete, the "{}bulk"{} elements}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01053}01053 have been created and are accessible via the various pointer-\/based }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01054}01054 access functions defined in the \(\backslash\)c Mesh class. Now we must}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01055}01055 create the prescribed-\/flux elements and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01056}01056 attach them to those "{}bulk"{} elements that have edges which coincide}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01057}01057 with the southern domain boundary (mesh boundary 1 in this example).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01058}01058 We use \(\backslash\)c Mesh member functions to determine}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01059}01059 -\/ the "{}bulk"{} elements that are located on that boundary,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01060}01060 -\/ the local coordinate of these elements that remains fixed along the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01061}01061 boundary, and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01062}01062 -\/ the value of the "{}fixed"{} local coordinate; in fact, this can only be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01063}01063 the maximum or minimum possible value.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01064}01064 .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01065}01065 \(\backslash\)code }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01066}01066 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01067}01067 // How many elements are adjacent to boundary 1?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01068}01068 unsigned b=1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01069}01069 unsigned n\_element=mesh\_pt()-\/>nboundary\_element(b);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01070}01070 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01071}01071 // Loop over the bulk elements on mesh boundary b:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01072}01072 for(unsigned e=0;e<n\_element;e++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01073}01073  \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01074}01074 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01075}01075   // Get pointer to the e-\/th bulk element on mesh boundary b. (Need to }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01076}01076   // recast to the specific bulk element type, because }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01077}01077   // boundary\_element\_pt() returns a pointer to a FiniteElement. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01078}01078   ELEMENT* bulk\_elem\_pt=dynamic\_cast<ELEMENT*>(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01079}01079    mesh\_pt()-\/>boundary\_element\_pt(b,e));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01080}01080   }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01081}01081   // Which local coordinate (in the bulk element) is constant}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01082}01082   // along the boundary?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01083}01083   unsigned s\_fixed\_index=mesh\_pt()-\/>s\_fixed\_index\_at\_boundary(b,e);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01084}01084 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01085}01085   // Is the constant coordinate fixed at its max. or min. value?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01086}01086   int s\_limit=mesh\_pt()-\/>s\_limit\_at\_boundary(b,e);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01087}01087 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01088}01088   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01089}01089 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01090}01090  Now we construct the \(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElements (templated by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01091}01091  the type of the bulk element). Their constructor takes a pointer to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01092}01092  the bulk element, and the information about the fixed local }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01093}01093  coordinate that we have just obtained from the \(\backslash\)c Mesh:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01094}01094 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01095}01095  \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01096}01096 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01097}01097   // Build the corresponding prescribed-\/flux element}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01098}01098   PoissonFluxElement<ELEMENT>* flux\_element\_pt = new }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01099}01099   PoissonFluxElement<ELEMENT>(bulk\_elem\_pt,s\_fixed\_index,s\_limit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01100}01100 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01101}01101   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01102}01102  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01103}01103   The constructor creates a prescribed-\/flux element with the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01104}01104   appropriate element geometry and sets its node pointers}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01105}01105   to the nodes on the appropriate face of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01106}01106   "{}bulk"{} element. We set the function pointer to the prescribed flux}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01107}01107   function -\/-\/ here assumed to be the function \(\backslash\)c get\_flux(...) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01108}01108   in the namespace \(\backslash\)c GlobalFunctions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01109}01109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01110}01110   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01111}01111 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01112}01112   // Set the pointer to the prescribed-\/flux function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01113}01113   flux\_element\_pt-\/>flux\_fct\_pt()=\&GlobalFunctions::get\_flux;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01114}01114 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01115}01115   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01116}01116 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01117}01117   Finally, we add the newly created element to the mesh:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01118}01118  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01119}01119   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01120}01120 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01121}01121   //Add the prescribed-\/flux element to the mesh}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01122}01122    mesh\_pt()-\/>add\_element\_pt(flux\_element\_pt);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01123}01123 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01124}01124  \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01125}01125 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01126}01126 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01127}01127 We still need to apply the Dirichlet boundary conditions on the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01128}01128 the remaining boundary nodes. This follows the usual pattern}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01129}01129 of looping over the boundary nodes and pinning their values, though}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01130}01130 we omit the nodes on boundary 1, because their values}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01131}01131 are unknown.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01132}01132 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01133}01133 \(\backslash\)code }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01134}01134 // Set the boundary conditions for this problem: All nodes are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01135}01135 // free by default -\/-\/ just pin the ones that have Dirichlet conditions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01136}01136 // here. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01137}01137 unsigned num\_bound = mesh\_pt()-\/>nboundary();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01138}01138 for (unsigned b=0;b<num\_bound;b++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01139}01139  \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01140}01140   //Leave nodes on boundary 1 free}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01141}01141   if (b!=1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01142}01142    \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01143}01143     unsigned num\_nod= mesh\_pt()-\/>nboundary\_node(b);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01144}01144     for (unsigned inod=0;inod<num\_nod;inod++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01145}01145      \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01146}01146       mesh\_pt()-\/>boundary\_node\_pt(b,inod)-\/>pin(0); }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01147}01147      \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01148}01148    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01149}01149  \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01150}01150 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01151}01151  [...]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01152}01152 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01153}01153 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01154}01154 \} // End of constructor}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01155}01155 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01156}01156 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01157}01157 [We have omitted the (standard) code for the assignment of the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01158}01158 linear solver, the assignment of equation numbers, etc.]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01159}01159 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01160}01160 The fine details of the procedure are embodied in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01161}01161 class definition of the \(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElements:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01162}01162 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01163}01163 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01164}01164 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01165}01165 //======================================================================\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01166}01166 \textcolor{comment}{/// \(\backslash\)short A class for elements that allow the imposition of a }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01167}01167 \textcolor{comment}{/// prescribed flux on the boundaries of Poisson elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01168}01168 \textcolor{comment}{/// The element geometry is obtained from the  FaceGeometry<ELEMENT> }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01169}01169 \textcolor{comment}{/// policy class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01170}01170 \textcolor{comment}{}//======================================================================}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01171}01171 template <class ELEMENT>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01172}01172 class PoissonFluxElement : public virtual FaceGeometry<ELEMENT>, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01173}01173 public virtual FaceElement}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01174}01174 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01175}01175 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01176}01176 public:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01177}01177 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01178}01178 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01179}01179 \textcolor{comment}{ /// \(\backslash\)short Constructor, takes the pointer to the "{}bulk"{} element, the }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01180}01180 \textcolor{comment}{ /// index of the fixed local coordinate and its value, represented}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01181}01181 \textcolor{comment}{ /// by an integer (+/-\/ 1), indicating that the face is located}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01182}01182 \textcolor{comment}{ /// at the max. or min. value of the "{}fixed"{} local coordinate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01183}01183 \textcolor{comment}{ /// in the bulk element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01184}01184 \textcolor{comment}{} PoissonFluxElement(FiniteElement* bulk\_el\_pt, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01185}01185                     const unsigned\& fixed\_local\_coord\_index, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01186}01186                     const int\& s\_limit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01187}01187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01188}01188 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01189}01189 [...]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01190}01190 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01191}01191 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01192}01192 \}; // End of class definition for PoissonFluxElement}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01193}01193 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01194}01194 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01195}01195 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01196}01196 \(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElements are }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01197}01197 derived from the \(\backslash\)c FaceGeometry class, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01198}01198 a policy class used to establish the geometry}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01199}01199 of the face element as a function of the "{}bulk"{} element }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01200}01200 specified by the template parameter. This inheritance structure}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01201}01201 is, in fact,  equivalent to the way in which \(\backslash\)c QPoissonElements}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01202}01202 are derived from geometric elements of the \(\backslash\)c QElement family.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01203}01203 The \(\backslash\)c FaceGeometry class should be }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01204}01204 defined for every conceivable type of "{}bulk"{} element but this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01205}01205 is usually a straightforward process. For}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01206}01206 "{}bulk"{} elements from the \(\backslash\)c QPoissonElement family, the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01207}01207 prescribed-\/flux elements have the same number of nodes along}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01208}01208 their 1D edges as their "{}bulk"{} elements but their spatial}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01209}01209 dimension is reduced by one. Hence, the complete class definition is:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01210}01210 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01211}01211 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01212}01212 //=======================================================================\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01213}01213 \textcolor{comment}{/// Face geometry for the QPoissonElement elements: The spatial }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01214}01214 \textcolor{comment}{/// dimension of the face elements is one lower than that of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01215}01215 \textcolor{comment}{/// bulk element but they have the same number of points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01216}01216 \textcolor{comment}{/// along their 1D edges.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01217}01217 \textcolor{comment}{}//=======================================================================}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01218}01218 template<unsigned DIM, unsigned NNODE\_1D>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01219}01219 class FaceGeometry<QPoissonElement<DIM,NNODE\_1D> >: }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01220}01220  public virtual QElement<DIM-\/1,NNODE\_1D>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01221}01221 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01222}01222 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01232}01232 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01233}01233 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01234}01234 hierher: probably need to handle the 0D case separately.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01235}01235 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01236}01236 This construction ensures that the number of nodes, etc., of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01237}01237 \(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElements is consistent with that of their}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01238}01238 higher-\/dimensional "{}bulk"{} elements. We now need to ensure that the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01239}01239 \(\backslash\)c PoissonFluxElement's node pointers refer to the (already existing)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01240}01240 nodes on the appropriate face of the "{}bulk"{} element. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01241}01241 The process is purely geometric, and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01242}01242 is performed by \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement::build\_face\_element(...) function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01243}01243 of the specific "{}bulk"{} geometric elements.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01244}01244 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01245}01245 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01246}01246 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01247}01247 //======================================================================\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01248}01248 \textcolor{comment}{/// Constructor, takes the pointer to the "{}bulk"{} element, the }}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01272}01272 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01273}01273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01274}01274 The constructor initially calls the constructor of the appropriate}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01275}01275 \(\backslash\)c FaceGeometry and thus establishes the element geometry. This is }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01276}01276 followed by a call to the \(\backslash\)c FaceElement constructor}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01277}01277 which allocates storage for any additional data that needs to be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01278}01278 stored on (generic) face elements. Finally, we call the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01279}01279 "{}bulk"{} element's \(\backslash\)c build\_face\_element() function to setup the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01280}01280 node pointers for the present (\(\backslash\)c this) element.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01281}01281 [\(\backslash\)b Note: \(\backslash\)c build\_face\_element() also assigns the additional data that is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01282}01282 stored in the \(\backslash\)c FaceElement base class. As mentioned above,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01283}01283 none of this information is required in the present context,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01284}01284 so we postpone the detailed discussion of this data to }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01285}01285 section ***FREE SURFACE NAVIER-\/STOKES ELEMENTS***.]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01286}01286 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01291}01291 \(\backslash\)subsection systems\_of\_PDEs Systems of PDEs: Multiple nodal values}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01292}01292 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01293}01293 So far, we have only considered scalar ODEs and PDEs but the finite}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01294}01294 element method can easily be extended to problems with }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01295}01295 vector-\/valued unknowns. As a simple example, we first consider a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01296}01296 system of 1D  Poisson equations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01297}01297 \(\backslash\)f[ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01298}01298 \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\}\string^2 u\_k(x)\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\} =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01299}01299 f\_k(x)  \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) for \$x\(\backslash\)in [0,1]\$  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01300}01300 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) subject to \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$u\_k(0) = g\_\{0k\}\$ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01301}01301 and \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$u\_k(1) = g\_\{1k\}\$, \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01302}01302 \(\backslash\)mbox\{\(\backslash\)hspace\{5cm\}\} \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01303}01303 where the coefficients \(\backslash\)f\$g\_\{0k\} \(\backslash\)f\$ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01304}01304 \(\backslash\)f\$g\_\{1k\}\(\backslash\)f\$ and the functions \(\backslash\)f\$ f\_k(x) \(\backslash\)f\$ are given, and }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01305}01305 \(\backslash\)f\$ k=1,...,K\(\backslash\)f\$.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01306}01306 Since the \(\backslash\)f\$ K \(\backslash\)f\$ ODEs have exactly the same form, we obtain}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01307}01307 \(\backslash\)f\$ K \(\backslash\)f\$ (identical) weak problems}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01308}01308 <CENTER>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01309}01309 <TABLE>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01310}01310 <TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01311}01311 <TD>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01312}01312 <CENTER>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01313}01313 <B> Problem P3 </B>\(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01314}01314 Find the functions  \(\backslash\)f\$ u\_k(x) \(\backslash\)in H(D) \(\backslash\)f\$ (where }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01315}01315 \(\backslash\)f\$ k=1,...,K\(\backslash\)f\$) that satisfy the essential boundary conditions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01316}01316 \(\backslash\)f[ u\_k(0) = g\_\{0k\} \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)mbox\{and\} \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)   u\_k(1) = g\_\{1k\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01317}01317 \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) for \$k=1,...,K\$,\} \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01318}01318 and for which}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01319}01319 \(\backslash\)f[ \(\backslash\)int\_0\string^1 \(\backslash\)left( \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} u\_k(x)\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\} \(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01320}01320 \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} \(\backslash\)phi\string^\{(test)\}(x)\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\} \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01321}01321 + f\_k(x) \(\backslash\)  \(\backslash\)phi\string^\{(test)\}(x) \(\backslash\)right)\(\backslash\)  dx = 0 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01322}01322 \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) for \$k=1,...,K\$,\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01323}01323 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01324}01324 for \(\backslash\)e all test functions  \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)phi\string^\{(test)\}(x) \(\backslash\)in H\_0(D). \(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01325}01325 </CENTER>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01326}01326 </TD>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01327}01327 </TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01328}01328 </TABLE>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01329}01329 </CENTER>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01330}01330 \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01331}01331 We expand all unknown functions in terms of the same (global) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01332}01332 shape functions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01333}01333 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01334}01334 u\string^\{(FE)\}\_k(x) = \(\backslash\)sum\_\{j=1\}\string^\{N\} U\_\{kj\} \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)psi\_j(x).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01335}01335 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01336}01336 Galerkin's method then yields the discrete residuals}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01337}01337   \(\backslash\)f[ r\_\{kj\} =  \(\backslash\)int\_0\string^1 \(\backslash\)left\(\backslash\)\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01338}01338   \(\backslash\)sum\_\{l=1\}\string^\{N\} U\_\{kl\} \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01339}01339   \(\backslash\)psi\_l(x)\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01340}01340   \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} \(\backslash\)psi\_j(x)\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\}\(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01341}01341   + f\_k(x) \(\backslash\)  \(\backslash\)psi\_j(x) \(\backslash\)right\(\backslash\)\} dx \(\backslash\)mbox\{\(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01342}01342   \(\backslash\) for \$i=2,...,N-\/1,\$ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) and \$k=1,...,K,\$  \} \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01343}01343 and, as before, we obtain one algebraic equation \(\backslash\)f\$r\_\{kj\} \(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01344}01344 for each of the \(\backslash\)f\$ (N-\/2)\(\backslash\)times K \(\backslash\)f\$ unknown coefficients}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01345}01345 \(\backslash\)f\$U\_\{kj\}\(\backslash\)f\$ whose values are not fixed by the boundary conditions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01346}01346 The finite element solution of these equations can easily be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01347}01347 derived by modifying algorithm @RA[P1\_Newton6]@ so that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01348}01348 -\/ every Node stores \(\backslash\)f\$ K \(\backslash\)f\$ values (rather than a single scalar).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01349}01349 -\/ the local and global equation numbering schemes are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01350}01350   modified to generate a linear numbering scheme for the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01351}01351   the doubly-\/indexed unknowns and equations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01352}01352 .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01353}01353 For this purpose we represent the (global) equation number }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01354}01354 of nodal value \(\backslash\)f\$ k \(\backslash\)f\$ at node \(\backslash\)f\$ j \(\backslash\)f\$ by \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)cal E\}(j,k)\(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01355}01355 and denote the number of nodal values that are stored at node \(\backslash\)f\$ j \(\backslash\)f\$ by }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01356}01356 \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)cal N\}(j)\(\backslash\)f\$.  As before, we reflect the fact that nodal }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01357}01357 values are pinned by setting their global equation number to -\/1. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01358}01358 The implementation only requires a few straightforward}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01359}01359 changes to Algorithm @RA[P1\_Newton6]@ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01360}01360 \(\backslash\)n \(\backslash\)n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01361}01361 <TABLE BORDER="{}1"{}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01362}01362 <TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01363}01363 <TD WIDTH="{}50\%"{} VALIGN="{}TOP"{}>}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01366}01366 -\/ Loop over all global nodes \(\backslash\)f\$ j \(\backslash\)f\$ that are located }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01558}01558                 \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)cal N\}(k\_\{local\}) \(\backslash\)f\$.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01559}01559                 </TD>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01560}01560                 </TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01561}01561                 </TABLE>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01562}01562               -\/ <TABLE BORDER=0>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01563}01563                 <TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01564}01564                 <TD bgcolor="{}cornsilk"{}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01565}01565                 Loop over the nodal values, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01566}01566                 \(\backslash\)f\$m=1,...,\{\(\backslash\)cal N\}(k\_\{local\})\(\backslash\)f\$: }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01567}01567                 </TD>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01568}01568                 </TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01569}01569                 </TABLE>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01570}01570                 -\/ Determine the global equation number }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01571}01571                 \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)cal E\}( k\_\{global\},m) \(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01572}01572                  -\/ If  \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)cal E\}( k\_\{global\},m) \(\backslash\)ne -\/1 \(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01573}01573                    -\/ Determine the local equation number from the element's}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01574}01574                      lookup scheme, \(\backslash\)f\$ j\_\{dof\} = \{\(\backslash\)cal L\}(k\_\{local\},m,e) \(\backslash\)f\$.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01575}01575                    -\/ Add the contribution to the element's Jacobian matrix}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01576}01576                      \(\backslash\)f[ J\_\{i\_\{dof\}j\_\{dof\}\}\string^\{(e)\} = }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01577}01577                          J\_\{i\_\{dof\}j\_\{dof\}\}\string^\{(e)\} + }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01578}01578                          \(\backslash\)left( }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01579}01579                          \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} \(\backslash\)psi\_\{k\_\{local\}\}\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\} \(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01580}01580                          \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} \(\backslash\)psi\_\{j\_\{local\}\}\}\{\(\backslash\)mbox\{d\} x\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01581}01581                          \(\backslash\)right)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01582}01582                          \(\backslash\)widehat\{\(\backslash\)cal J\} \(\backslash\) W\_\{i\_\{int\}\}  \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01583}01583                   .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01584}01584                 .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01585}01585               .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01586}01586             .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01587}01587           .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01588}01588         .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01589}01589       .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01590}01590     .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01591}01591     \(\backslash\)n  \(\backslash\)n   }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01592}01592 </TD>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01593}01593 </TR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01594}01594 </TABLE>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01595}01595 \(\backslash\)n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01596}01596 Again, the modifications are straightforward. At each node}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01597}01597 we loop over the multiple nodal values; furthermore, we have added an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01598}01598 additional index to the local equation numbering scheme, so that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01599}01599 \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)cal L\}(j\_\{local\},k,e)\(\backslash\)f\$ stores the local equation number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01600}01600 of the \(\backslash\)f\$k\(\backslash\)f\$-\/th value at local node  \(\backslash\)f\$j\_\{local\}\(\backslash\)f\$ in element \(\backslash\)f\$e\(\backslash\)f\$.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01601}01601 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01602}01602 The example considered here is, of course, very simple. In fact, the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01603}01603 \(\backslash\)f\$ K \(\backslash\)f\$ ODEs in Problem P3 are uncoupled and could (should!) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01604}01604 have been solved independently. However, the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01605}01605 algorithms developed above can be applied to any systems }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01606}01606 of PDEs in which the \(\backslash\)f\$ K \(\backslash\)f\$ differential operators have the same form. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01607}01607 A more practically relevant example is given by the 3D Navier-\/Lame }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01608}01608 equations of linear elasticity:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01609}01609 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01610}01610 \(\backslash\)sum\_\{k=1\}\string^3  \(\backslash\)left[ (\(\backslash\)lambda+\(\backslash\)mu) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01611}01611 \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 u\_k\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_k\(\backslash\)partial x\_i\} + }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01612}01612 \(\backslash\)mu \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 u\_i\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_k\string^2\} \(\backslash\)right]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01613}01613 + F\_i =0 \(\backslash\)mbox\{\(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$(i=1,...,3)\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01614}01614 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01615}01615 The local equation numbering scheme for these equations is }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01616}01616 identical to that for Problem P3 shown above. Only the computation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01617}01617 of the element's residual vector and Jacobian matrix must  be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01618}01618 changed. This is left as an exercise. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01619}01619 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01620}01620 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01621}01621 <B>Implementation</B> \(\backslash\)n\(\backslash\)n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01622}01622 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01623}01623 To allow the object-\/oriented implementation of the above}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01624}01624 algorithms, each Node stores its nodal values in a vector. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01625}01625 The number of values that need to be stored at the Node}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01626}01626 is provided as an argument to its constructor.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01627}01627 The argument to the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01628}01628 \(\backslash\)c Node::value\_pt(...) function identifies}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01629}01629 individual nodal values:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01630}01630 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01631}01631 unsigned i\_value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01632}01632 double nodal\_value = *(Node::value\_pt(i\_value));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01633}01633 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01634}01634 The Node object has a member function that returns the number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01635}01635 of values stored,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01636}01636 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01637}01637 unsigned nvalues = Node::nvalue();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01638}01638 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01639}01639 and the global equation numbers of the individual nodal values }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01640}01640 are accessible via a Node member function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01641}01641 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01642}01642 unsigned i\_value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01643}01643 unsigned i\_eqn = Node::eqn\_number(i\_value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01644}01644 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01645}01645 Finally, the nodal values' pinned status can be obtained from}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01646}01646 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01647}01647 unsigned i\_value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01648}01648 bool pinned = Node::is\_pinned(i\_value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01649}01649 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01650}01650 and nodal values are pinned/unpinned with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01651}01651 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01652}01652 unsigned i\_value,j\_value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01653}01653 Node::pin(i\_value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01654}01654 Node::unpin(j\_value);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01655}01655 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01656}01656 This finally provides the explanation for the mysterious argument}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01657}01657 that we had to provide to these functions in all previous}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01658}01658 examples: In a scalar problem, each Node only stores a single}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01659}01659 value whose index is "{}0"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01660}01660 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01661}01661   One question still needs to be addressed, however. Nodes are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01662}01662 usually created during the Mesh generation process. How does the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01663}01663 Mesh constructor "{}know"{} how many values a given Node should store? }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01664}01664 Also, what should the spatial dimension of the newly created Node be?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01665}01665 (Note that the spatial dimension of a Node is not necessarily the same}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01666}01666 as that of the Mesh: For instance, a 1D Mesh can be used to }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01667}01667 discretise a spatially one-\/dimensional Poisson equation, in which}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01668}01668 case each node must store a single (Eulerian) coordinate.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01669}01669 However, the same Mesh could also be used to discretise a }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01670}01670 one-\/dimensional structural object, such as a beam, in a 3D Eulerian }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01671}01671 space, in which case each Node needs to store three (Eulerian)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01672}01672 coordinates. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01673}01673 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01674}01674 The example considered above shows that the number of }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01675}01675 values that are "{}required"{} at a given Node is determined by the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01676}01676 system of equations that is being solved. This information becomes }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01677}01677 available when a specific system of equations is implemented in a specific}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01678}01678 FiniteElement. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01679}01679 The FiniteElement class therefore provides the pure virtual member function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01680}01680 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01681}01681 FiniteElement::required\_nvalue(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01682}01682 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01683}01683 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01684}01684 which returns the number of values required at a given local Node}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01685}01685 in the element. This function should be implemented for every specific}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01686}01686 FiniteElement. For a Poisson element (or any other element that implements}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01687}01687 the discretisation of a scalar PDE), the function should return 1; for an }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01688}01688 element that discretises the 3D Navier-\/Lame equations, the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01689}01689 should return 3; etc. Note that our implementation allows the possibility}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01690}01690 that different Nodes in an element require storage for different}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01691}01691 numbers of values, see \(\backslash\)ref mixed\_interpolation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01692}01692 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01693}01693 The required spatial dimension of the Node is, again, determined by each}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01694}01694 specific element and should be specified by calling the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01695}01695 protected member function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01696}01696 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01697}01697 FiniteElement::set\_nodal\_dimension(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01698}01698 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01699}01699 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01700}01700 For instance, for an element that solves the 2D Poisson equation, this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01701}01701 function must be called in the constructor with argument 2. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01702}01702 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01703}01703 Using the element-\/specific information provided by these }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01704}01704 virtual FiniteElement member functions, the construction of a Node }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01705}01705 of the appropriate type can be performed by the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01706}01706 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01707}01707 FiniteElement::construct\_node(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01708}01708 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01709}01709 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01710}01710 This function performs the following tasks:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01711}01711 -\/ it creates a new Node, determining the arguments to the Node}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01712}01712   constructor (spatial dimension, number of values, etc) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01713}01713   from the FiniteElement member functions just discussed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01714}01714 -\/ it stores a pointer to the newly created Node in the element's}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01715}01715   own lookup scheme.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01716}01716 -\/ it returns a pointer to the newly created Node so that it can be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01717}01717   added to the Mesh's storage scheme for Nodes. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01718}01718 .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01719}01719 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01720}01720 Here is a code fragment that illustrates the creation of Nodes during}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01721}01721 the mesh generation process. (Recall that specific Meshes are usually }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01722}01722 templated by the element type, so that a Mesh that was originally }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01723}01723 developed for the solution of a Poisson equation can also be used to }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01724}01724 solve the Navier-\/Stokes equations, say).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01725}01725 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01726}01726 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01727}01727 template<class ELEMENT>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01728}01728 class SomeMesh : public Mesh}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01729}01729 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01730}01730 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01731}01731  public:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01732}01732 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01733}01733 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Mesh constructor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01734}01734 \textcolor{comment}{}  SomeMesh()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01735}01735    \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01736}01736 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01737}01737      // Create the first element (Note that element constructors }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01738}01738      // never have any arguments, therefore this works}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01739}01739      // for any type of element!)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01740}01740      ELEMENT* el\_pt=new ELEMENT;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01741}01741 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01742}01742      // Add the (pointer to the) element to the Mesh's Element\_pt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01743}01743      // vector}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01744}01744      Element\_pt.push\_back(new ELEMENT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01745}01745 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01746}01746      // How many nodes does the element have?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01747}01747      unsigned nnod=element\_pt-\/>nnode();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01748}01748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01749}01749      // Loop over the nodes (we're creating the first element}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01750}01750      // so all nodes are new)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01751}01751      for (unsigned j=0;j<nnod;j++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01752}01752        \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01753}01753         // Create the element's j-\/th local node,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01754}01754         // using the parameters (spatial dimension, number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01755}01755         // of values, etc) specified by  FiniteElement::required\_ndim(...),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01756}01756         // FiniteElement::required\_nvalue(...), etc.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01757}01757         // Also store a pointer to the newly created Node}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01758}01758         // in the element's own lookup scheme for nodes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01759}01759         Node* nod\_pt=element\_pt-\/>construct\_node(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01760}01760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01761}01761         // Add the newly created node to the Mesh's own storage scheme}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01762}01762         Node\_pt.push\_back(nod\_pt);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01763}01763        \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01764}01764 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01765}01765 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01766}01766       // Now do the subsequent elements}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01767}01767 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01768}01768       [...]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01769}01769 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01770}01770 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01771}01771       // Assign the nodal coordinates}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01772}01772 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01773}01773       [...]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01774}01774 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01775}01775    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01776}01776 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01777}01777 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01778}01778 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01779}01779 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01780}01780  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01781}01781 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01782}01782 <HR>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01783}01783 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01784}01784 \(\backslash\)subsection mixed\_interpolation Mixed interpolation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01785}01785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01786}01786 In the examples considered so far, each equation in the system of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01787}01787 PDEs had the same structure and it was }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01788}01788 natural to use the same interpolation for all unknowns}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01789}01789 and the same test functions for each PDE in the system. However, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01790}01790 there are many systems of PDEs whose constituent equations }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01791}01791 have different structures. As an example, we consider the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01792}01792 steady 2D Navier-\/Stokes equations, which comprise the two momentum equations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01793}01793 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01794}01794 Re \(\backslash\)sum\_\{k=1\}\string^2  u\_k  \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial u\_i\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_k\} +}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01795}01795 \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial p\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_i\} -\/  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01796}01796 \(\backslash\)sum\_\{k=1\}\string^2 \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 u\_i\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_k\string^2\} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01797}01797  =0 \(\backslash\)mbox\{\(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$(i=1,...,2)\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01798}01798 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01799}01799 and the continuity equation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01800}01800 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01801}01801 \(\backslash\)sum\_\{k=1\}\string^2  \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial u\_k\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_k\} =0.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01802}01802 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01803}01803 The structure of the momentum equations differs from }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01804}01804 that of the continuity equation. Furthermore, the equations contain }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01805}01805 second derivatives of the two velocity components, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01806}01806 \(\backslash\)f\$ u\_i \(\backslash\) (i=1,...2),\(\backslash\)f\$ but only first derivatives of the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01807}01807 pressure, \(\backslash\)f\$p\(\backslash\)f\$. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01808}01808 This raises two important questions:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01809}01809 -\/ How should we define the weak form for this coupled problem? Should}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01810}01810   we use the same class of test functions for both types of equations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01811}01811   or should we use a different class for each one?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01812}01812 -\/ How should we represent the two types of unknowns? Should we use}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01813}01813   the same basis functions for the pressure and the velocity or should}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01814}01814   we use a different type of interpolation for each one?}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01815}01815 . }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01816}01816 For a general system of PDEs, these are difficult questions which can only}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01817}01817 be answered by careful analysis of the governing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01818}01818 equations. Luckily, in the case of the Navier-\/Stokes equations,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01819}01819 the analysis is well-\/established and we refer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01820}01820 to the standard literature [e.g. P.M. Gresho and R.L. Sani:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01821}01821 "{}Incompressible Flow and the Finite Element Method"{} Vol. 1 and 2.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01822}01822 Wiley (2000)] which provides several possible answers to these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01823}01823 questions. "{}Equal-\/order interpolations"{}, in which the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01824}01824 same shape functions are used to represent the pressure}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01825}01825 and the velocity components, are generally found to result}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01826}01826 in unstable elements. Most stable discretisations are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01827}01827 based on "{}mixed interpolations"{} in which the velocity components are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01828}01828 represented by one set of basis functions,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01829}01829 \(\backslash\)f[ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01830}01830 u\_i(x\_k) = \(\backslash\)sum\_\{j=1\}\string^N U\_\{ij\} \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)psi\_j(x\_k),\(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)  (8)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01831}01831 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01832}01832 and another set of basis functions, \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)psi\string^\{(P)\}\_j(x\_k) \(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l01833}01833 (j=1,...,N\_P)\(\backslash\)f\$,  is employed to approximate the pressure}
