\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03017}03017  \(\backslash\)delta X\_\{km\}  =0. \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)  (36)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03018}03018  \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03019}03019 [Note that summation convention enforces the summation over the index }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03020}03020 \(\backslash\)f\$ k \(\backslash\)f\$.]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03021}03021 The displacement boundary condition (19)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03022}03022 determines the positions of all nodes that are located on the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03023}03023 boundary \(\backslash\)f\$A\_\{displ\}\(\backslash\)f\$, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03024}03024 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03025}03025  X\_\{ij\} = R\string^\{(BC)\}\_i(\(\backslash\)Xi\_\{lj\}) \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) if node \$j\$ is }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03026}03026  located on \$A\_\{displ\},\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03027}03027 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03028}03028 and equation (21) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03029}03029 requires their variations to vanish,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03030}03030 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03031}03031  \(\backslash\)delta X\_\{ij\} = 0 \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) if node \$j\$ is located on \$A\_\{displ\}.\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03032}03032 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03033}03033 The variations of all other nodal positions are arbitrary (and independent}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03034}03034 of each other), therefore the terms in the curly brackets in }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03035}03035 (36) need to vanish individually. This provides one }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03036}03036 (discrete) equation for each unknown \(\backslash\)f\$X\_\{km\}\(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03037}03037  \(\backslash\)f[ f\_\{km\} = }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03038}03038   \(\backslash\)int \(\backslash\)left[ \(\backslash\)sigma\string^\{ij\} \(\backslash\) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03039}03039   \(\backslash\)left(\(\backslash\)sum\_\{k=1\}\string^N X\_\{kl\} \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial \(\backslash\)psi\_l\}\{\(\backslash\)partial \(\backslash\)xi\string^i\} \(\backslash\)right)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03040}03040        \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial \(\backslash\)psi\_m\}\{\(\backslash\)partial \(\backslash\)xi\string^j\} \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03041}03041       -\/ \(\backslash\)left( f\_k -\/ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03042}03042   \(\backslash\)Lambda\string^2 \(\backslash\)left(\(\backslash\)sum\_\{k=1\}\string^N}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03043}03043     \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 X\_\{kl\}\}\{\(\backslash\)partial t\string^2\} \(\backslash\)psi\_l \(\backslash\)right) \(\backslash\)right) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03044}03044  \(\backslash\)psi\_m \(\backslash\)right] \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)Gamma \(\backslash\) dv \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03045}03045  -\/ \(\backslash\)oint\_\{A\_\{tract\}\} t\_k \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)psi\_m \(\backslash\) dA }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03046}03046   =0. \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)  \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (37)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03047}03047  \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03048}03048 These equations can again be assembled in an element-\/by-\/element}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03049}03049 fashion.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03050}03050 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03051}03051 \(\backslash\)subsubsection solid\_implementation Implementation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03052}03052 We will now discuss how the discrete equations (37) are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03053}03053 implemented in \(\backslash\)c oomph-\/lib. To facilitate the analysis}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03054}03054 of multi-\/physics problems, we introduce generalisations of the \(\backslash\)c Node, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03055}03055 \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement and \(\backslash\)c Mesh classes which provide}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03056}03056 separate storage (and access functions) for all solid mechanics}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03057}03057 Data. The resulting \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements can }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03058}03058 be used as stand-\/alone elements for the simulation of }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03059}03059 pure solid mechanics problems. More importantly, however, the design}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03060}03060 makes it easy to employ multiple inheritance to create }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03061}03061 more complex elements that solve the equations of solid mechanics}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03062}03062 together with }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03063}03063 any other field equations. For instance, if we combine}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03064}03064 a \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement that solves the unsteady heat equation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03065}03065 with an \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement that describes the elastic }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03066}03066 deformations, we obtain an element that can be used to simulate }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03067}03067 unsteady heat conduction in an elastic body that performs }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03068}03068 large-\/amplitude oscillations, say.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03069}03069 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03070}03070 <CENTER> <B>The SolidNode class:</B></CENTER> }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03071}03071 The class \(\backslash\)c SolidNode is derived from \(\backslash\)c Node and }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03072}03072 implements the additional functionality required for solid}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03073}03073 mechanics problems. The key new feature is that each Node}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03074}03074 needs to store its (fixed) Lagrangian coordinate \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)Xi\_\{ij\}\(\backslash\)f\$,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03075}03075 while its Eulerian position  \(\backslash\)f\$ X\_\{ij\}\(\backslash\)f\$ needs to be regarded}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03076}03076 as an unknown. This requires the following changes to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03077}03077 member functions of the \(\backslash\)c Node class:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03078}03078 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03079}03079 -\/ The function \(\backslash\)c Node::x(...) returns the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03080}03080   Eulerian coordinates of the \(\backslash\)c Node. Internally, this function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03081}03081   accesses the nodal coordinates via pointers to double}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03082}03082   precision numbers. This data structure is adequate for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03083}03083   problems in which the nodal positions are either known a priori }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03084}03084   or determined by an algebraic node update function. However, the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03085}03085   scheme does not allow us to regard the nodal positions as}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03086}03086   unknowns -\/-\/ as required by our expansion}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03087}03087   (35). In \(\backslash\)c SolidNodes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03088}03088   the nodal positions are therefore stored as \(\backslash\)c Data (whose }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03089}03089   values can either be unknowns or pinned values, and which can have a time}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03090}03090   history). We overload the \(\backslash\)c Node::x(...) function by }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03091}03091   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03092}03092   SolidNode::x(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03093}03093   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03094}03094   which returns the (now variable) Eulerian nodal position of the node.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03095}03095   The function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03096}03096   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03097}03097   SolidNode::position\_eqn\_number(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03098}03098   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03099}03099   gives access to the global equation number for each}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03100}03100   nodal coordinate and, following our usual convention, the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03101}03101   returns -\/1 if a coordinate is pinned.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03102}03102 -\/ We introduce a new member function }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03103}03103   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03104}03104   SolidNode::xi(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03105}03105   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03106}03106   which returns the (fixed) Lagrangian coordinates of the node.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03107}03107 -\/ Both functions have the usual extensions to generalised}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03108}03108   coordinates}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03109}03109   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03110}03110   SolidNode::x\_gen(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03111}03111   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03112}03112   and }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03113}03113   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03114}03114   SolidNode::xi\_gen(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03115}03115   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03116}03116   which are required for Hermite elements and any other elements}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03117}03117   that use generalised nodal coordinates to interpolate the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03118}03118   element's geometry.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03119}03119 -\/ Similar to the \(\backslash\)c Data member function \(\backslash\)c Data::pin(...) which can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03120}03120   be used to pin specific nodal values, we provide the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03121}03121   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03122}03122   SolidNode::position\_pin(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03123}03123   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03124}03124   which allows pinning of selected nodal coordinates.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03125}03125 -\/ Dynamic problems require the evaluation of time-\/derivatives}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03126}03126   of the nodal positions, such as \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)partial\string^2 X\_\{ij\}/\(\backslash\)partial t\string^2\(\backslash\)f\$,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03127}03127   see (37). These time-\/derivatives are evaluated by the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03128}03128   \(\backslash\)c TimeStepper of the positional \(\backslash\)c Data.  By default,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03129}03129   we use the same \(\backslash\)c TimeStepper for the nodal \(\backslash\)c Data and for the nodal }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03130}03130   positions. In multi-\/physics problems this might not be }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03131}03131   appropriate. Consider, for instance, solving an unsteady }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03132}03132   heat equation in a dynamically deforming, elastic body. In this problem}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03133}03133   the 2nd time-\/derivatives of the nodal position might be evaluated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03134}03134   by a \(\backslash\)c Newmark scheme, acting on the history values of the nodal}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03135}03135   positions, whereas the time-\/derivatives of the temperature}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03136}03136   might be determined by a \(\backslash\)c BDF scheme, operating on the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03137}03137   history values of the nodal \(\backslash\)c Data.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03138}03138   In such cases, the default assignment for the two timesteppers }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03139}03139   can be overwritten with the access functions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03140}03140   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03141}03141   SolidNode::position\_time\_stepper\_pt()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03142}03142   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03143}03143   and }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03144}03144   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03145}03145   SolidNode::time\_stepper\_pt()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03146}03146   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03147}03147   where the latter is inherited from \(\backslash\)c Data::time\_stepper\_pt().}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03148}03148 -\/ Our implementation is based on the displacement form of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03149}03149   principle of virtual displacements in which the position vector }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03150}03150   \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i) \(\backslash\)f\$ in the deformed configuration is regarded}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03151}03151   as the unknown vector field. Equation  (35)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03152}03152   defines the representation of this vector}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03153}03153   field within each finite element in terms of the nodal coordinates.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03154}03154   Some constitutive equations require the representation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03155}03155   of additional (non-\/positional) variables.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03156}03156   For instance, for incompressible (or nearly incompressible) materials,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03157}03157   the stress \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)sigma\string^\{ij\} \(\backslash\)f\$ contains a contribution from the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03158}03158   (scalar) pressure field \(\backslash\)f\$ p \(\backslash\)f\$; see the discussion of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03159}03159   constitutive equations above. If we choose a continuous}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03160}03160   representation for the pressure in which its value is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03161}03161   interpolated between nodal values (as in Taylor-\/Hood-\/type}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03162}03162   elements), the nodal pressure values could in principle be stored}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03163}03163   in the "{}normal"{} nodal Data. However, to retain a clear }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03164}03164   distinction between}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03165}03165   solid-\/mechanics and non-\/solid-\/mechanics quantities we store}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03166}03166   such "{}additional nodal solid values"{} in their own \(\backslash\)c Data object }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03167}03167   to which we provide access with the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03168}03168   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03169}03169   SolidNode::additional\_solid\_data\_pt()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03170}03170   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03171}03171   As with all other nodal quantities, the number of additional }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03172}03172   solid data values, needs to be specified as an argument to the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03173}03173   \(\backslash\)c SolidNode constructor when the \(\backslash\)c SolidNode is created.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03174}03174   The access function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03175}03175   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03176}03176   SolidNode::nadditional\_solid\_value()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03177}03177   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03178}03178   returns the number of additional solid values that are stored}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03179}03179   at an \(\backslash\)c SolidNode; the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03180}03180   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03181}03181   SolidNode::additional\_solid\_eqn\_number(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03182}03182   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03183}03183   returns the global equation number of the SolidNode's }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03184}03184   additional solid values, and there are further member functions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03185}03185   that allow pinning/unpinning of these values, etc.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03186}03186 -\/ Finally, \(\backslash\)c SolidNodes overload the function }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03187}03187   \(\backslash\)c Data::assign\_eqn\_numbers()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03188}03188   with }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03189}03189   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03190}03190   SolidNode::assign\_eqn\_numbers()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03191}03191   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03192}03192   which creates global equation numbers for all (non-\/pinned) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03193}03193   positional values and any additional (nodal) solid values, and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03194}03194   then deals with the "{}normal"{} nodal Data by calling}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03195}03195   \(\backslash\)c Data::assign\_eqn\_numbers().}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03196}03196 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03197}03197 <CENTER><B>The SolidFiniteElement class:</B></CENTER>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03198}03198 The class \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement is derived from \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement and }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03199}03199 implements the additional functionality required for solid}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03200}03200 mechanics problems. Again, most of the additional (or revised)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03201}03201 functionality is related to the presence of the two coordinate}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03202}03202 systems which requires the following changes to \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03203}03203 member functions:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03204}03204 -\/ The nodes of \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements are \(\backslash\)c SolidNodes, therefore}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03205}03205   we overload the function \(\backslash\)c FiniteElements::construct\_node(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03206}03206   to ensure that an \(\backslash\)c SolidNode with the appropriate }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03207}03207   amount of storage is built. As in the case of \(\backslash\)c FiniteElements, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03208}03208   the required spatial dimension of the elements' constituent }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03209}03209   nodes, their number of nodal values etc. are specified via}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03210}03210   the \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement's (pure) virtual member functions }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03211}03211   \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement::required\_ndim(...),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03212}03212   \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement::required\_nvalue(...), etc, which need to be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03213}03213   implemented for all specific elements that are derived from}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03214}03214   the \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement base class.  As discussed above, the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03215}03215   constructor of the \(\backslash\)c SolidNodes requires additional parameters, such}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03216}03216   as the number of Lagrangian coordinates. These need to be specified }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03217}03217   by implementing \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement::required\_nlagrangian(...) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03218}03218   and similar other functions. As in the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03219}03219   case of \(\backslash\)c FiniteElements, many of these functions are already}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03220}03220   implemented as virtual (rather than pure virtual) functions which provide}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03221}03221   sensible default values. For instance, by default, the number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03222}03222   of additional nodal solid values is set to zero, etc. Such}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03223}03223   functions need to be overloaded in specific derived elements}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03224}03224   if the default values are not appropriate.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03225}03225 -\/ The interpolation of the Eulerian coordinates, implemented}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03226}03226   in \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement::interpolated\_x(...), can remain unchanged}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03227}03227   because of the way in which we have overloaded \(\backslash\)c Node::x(...) with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03228}03228   SolidNode::x(...). \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements provide additional}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03229}03229   functions, such as }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03230}03230   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03231}03231   SolidFiniteElement::interpolated\_xi(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03232}03232   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03233}03233   which determines the interpolated Lagrangian coordinates at}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03234}03234   a specified local coordinate within the element, or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03235}03235   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03236}03236   SolidFiniteElement::xi(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03237}03237   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03238}03238   which provides a wrapper for the nodal values of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03239}03239   Lagrangian coordinates. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03240}03240 -\/ The displacement form of the principle of virtual displacements }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03241}03241   (37) contains derivatives of the shape functions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03242}03242   with respect to the Lagrangian (rather than the Eulerian)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03243}03243   coordinates. Their computation is implemented in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03244}03244   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03245}03245   SolidFiniteElement::dshape\_lagrangian(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03246}03246   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03247}03247 -\/ We have already discussed the need to represent}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03248}03248   additional, non-\/positional solid variables (such as pressures)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03249}03249   within an \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement. The storage }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03250}03250   of the "{}additional solid values"{} at the \(\backslash\)c SolidNodes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03251}03251   allows a globally continuous representation of such variables}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03252}03252   (similar to the continuous pressure representation in Taylor-\/Hood}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03253}03253   elements). Discontinuous representations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03254}03254   (as in Crouzeix-\/Raviart elements) require the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03255}03255   storage of additional internal solid variables. In principle, these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03256}03256   could again be stored in the \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement's internal Data}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03257}03257   but for the reasons outlined at the beginning of this section, }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03258}03258   we store \(\backslash\)e all solid variables in separate Data items.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03259}03259   The function }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03260}03260   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03261}03261   SolidFiniteElement::internal\_solid\_data\_pt(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03262}03262   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03263}03263   provides access to the additional internal solid \(\backslash\)c Data.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03264}03264   The total number of \(\backslash\)c Data items stored as }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03265}03265   internal solid \(\backslash\)c Data  can be obtained from }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03266}03266   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03267}03267   SolidFiniteElement::ninternal\_solid\_data() }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03268}03268   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03269}03269 -\/ We have now created storage and access functions for all the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03270}03270   additional \(\backslash\)c Data that is required for solid mechanics problems: }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03271}03271   -\/ Data that represents the nodal positions,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03272}03272   -\/ Data that represents additional, non-\/positional nodal Data}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03273}03273     such as continuously interpolated pressures, and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03274}03274   -\/ Data that represents additional internal Data, used, e.g.,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03275}03275     to represent discontinuously interpolated pressures.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03276}03276   .}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03277}03277   We need to ensure that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03278}03278   these Data items are included in the various equation numbering}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03279}03279   schemes. This only requires overloading of }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03280}03280   \(\backslash\)c FiniteElement::assign\_internal\_eqn\_numbers(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03281}03281   with a version that also sets up the global equation numbers}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03282}03282   for the additional internal solid values. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03283}03283   Furthermore, we provide the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03284}03284   \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement::assign\_solid\_local\_eqn\_numbers() }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03285}03285   which sets up the local equation numbering scheme for all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03286}03286   solid Data associated with an element. This function will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03287}03287   called from the overloaded }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03288}03288   \(\backslash\)c SolidMesh::assign\_local\_eqn\_numbers()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03289}03289   function to be discussed in the next section.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03290}03290 -\/ We're done! \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements now form a suitable basis for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03291}03291   all elements whose deformation is determined}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03292}03292   by the equations of solid mechanics (or some variant thereof). }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03293}03293   To implement a specific}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03294}03294   solid mechanics element, we need to represent its geometry,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03295}03295   its state of stress, etc., in terms of the \(\backslash\)c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03296}03296   SolidFiniteElement's nodal and additional internal solid}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03297}03297   \(\backslash\)c Data. This requires the specification of the shape functions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03298}03298   and the functions that compute the element's Jacobian matrix}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03299}03299   and its residual vector -\/-\/ the latter implementing the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03300}03300   element's contribution to the global residual vector defined by the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03301}03301   discretised principle of virtual displacements, (37).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03302}03302   As for "{}normal"{} \(\backslash\)c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03303}03303   FiniteElements it is sensible to construct specific \(\backslash\)c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03304}03304   SolidFiniteElements in a hierarchy which separates between}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03305}03305   the implementation of the governing equations and the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03306}03306   representation of the element geometry. For instance,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03307}03307   the \(\backslash\)c SolidQElement family represents the generalisation of the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03308}03308   \(\backslash\)c QElement family to \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements, while \(\backslash\)c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03309}03309   PVDEquations implement the principle of virtual}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03310}03310   displacements (37). The two are combined}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03311}03311   by multiple inheritance to form the \(\backslash\)c QPVDElement class.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03312}03312 -\/ The computation of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03313}03313   element's Jacobian matrix requires the evaluation of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03314}03314   the derivatives of the discrete residuals (37) with respect}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03315}03315   to the unknown nodal positions, and with respect to any}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03316}03316   additional unknown solid mechanics variables (e.g. pressures). The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03317}03317   derivatives with respect to the nodal positions result in }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03318}03318   fairly complex algebraic expressions and in our experience it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03319}03319   is more efficient to evaluate these entries by finite}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03320}03320   differencing. This operation is completely generic}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03321}03321   and is implemented in }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03322}03322   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03323}03323   SolidFiniteElement::get\_jacobian(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03324}03324   \(\backslash\)endcode }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03325}03325   It is therefore not necessary to implement this function for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03326}03326   \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements that only involve positional degrees of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03327}03327   freedom (unless the setup of the element's Jacobian matrix }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03328}03328   by finite differencing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03329}03329   is deemed to be too inefficient -\/-\/ however, as stated above, we very much}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03330}03330   doubt that its analytical computation would be faster). }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03331}03331   An example is given by the \(\backslash\)c SolidEquations class in which}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03332}03332   only the function \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement::get\_residual(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03333}03333   is implemented -\/-\/ the element's Jacobian matrix for }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03334}03334   \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements that are derived from these equations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03335}03335   is computed automatically by the finite differencing operations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03336}03336   implemented in \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement::get\_jacobian(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03337}03337   \(\backslash\)n \(\backslash\)n}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03338}03338   \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements that involve non-\/positional degrees}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03339}03339   of freedom can still call this function to compute the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03340}03340   entries that correspond to derivatives with respect to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03341}03341   the nodal positions. Any other entries (such as the derivatives}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03342}03342   of the residuals with respect to the solid pressure degrees}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03343}03343   of freedom) need to be computed separately. The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03344}03344   \(\backslash\)c SolidEquationsWithPressure class provides an example for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03345}03345   this approach.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03346}03346 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03347}03347 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03348}03348 <CENTER><B> The SolidMesh class: </B></CENTER>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03349}03349 Finally, we introduce the \(\backslash\)c SolidMesh class as a generalisation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03350}03350 of the \(\backslash\)c Mesh class. The key features of this class are:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03351}03351 -\/ It overloads the \(\backslash\)c Mesh::node\_pt(...) function with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03352}03352   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03353}03353   SolidMesh::node\_pt(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03354}03354   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03355}03355   which returns a pointer to an \(\backslash\)c SolidNode, rather than a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03356}03356   "{}normal"{} \(\backslash\)c Node. Equivalent access functions are implemented for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03357}03357   all other \(\backslash\)c Mesh member functions that return pointers to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03358}03358   \(\backslash\)c Nodes.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03359}03359 -\/ It overloads the \(\backslash\)c Mesh::assign\_local\_eqn\_numbers()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03360}03360   function with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03361}03361   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03362}03362   SolidMesh::assign\_local\_eqn\_numbers(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03363}03363   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03364}03364   This function calls the elements' "{}normal"{} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03365}03365   \(\backslash\)c GeneralisedElement::assign\_local\_eqn\_numbers() function,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03366}03366   followed by a call to  }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03367}03367   \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement::assign\_solid\_local\_eqn\_numbers(),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03368}03368   which implements the local equation numbering for the }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03369}03369   solid mechanics degrees of freedom. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03370}03370 -\/ Finally, we provide the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03371}03371   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03372}03372   SolidMesh::set\_lagrangian\_nodal\_coordinates()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03373}03373   \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03374}03374   which assigns the current Eulerian coordinates of all \(\backslash\)c Nodes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03375}03375   to their Lagrangian coordinates, thus turning the current}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03376}03376   configuration into the reference configuration). This function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03377}03377   greatly facilitates the construction of \(\backslash\)c SolidMeshes via}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03378}03378   inheritance from existing \(\backslash\)c Meshes. If, for instance, \(\backslash\)c SomeMesh}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03379}03379   is an existing, fully functional \(\backslash\)c Mesh, the corresponding}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03380}03380   \(\backslash\)c SolidMesh can be constructed with a few lines}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03381}03381   of code, as in this example:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03382}03382   \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03383}03383   //=================================================================}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03384}03384   // SolidMesh version of SomeMesh}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03416}03416  \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03417}03417 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03418}03418 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03419}03419 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03420}03420 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03421}03421 \(\backslash\)subsubsection Solid\_IC Timestepping and the generation of initial conditions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03422}03422 In time-\/dependent problems, the boundary value problem defined by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03423}03423 the variational principle (28) needs to be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03424}03424 augmented by suitable initial conditions which specify the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03425}03425 state of the system at time \(\backslash\)f\$ t=t\_0. \(\backslash\)f\$ The initial}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03426}03426 conditions specify the initial shape of the solid body,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03427}03427 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03428}03428 \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i,t=t\_0) =  \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}\string^\{(IC)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03429}03429 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (38)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03430}03430 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03431}03431 and its initial velocity,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03432}03432 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03433}03433 \(\backslash\)left. \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i,t)\}\{\(\backslash\)partial t\} \(\backslash\)right|\_\{t=t\_0\} = }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03434}03434 \{\(\backslash\)bf V\}\string^\{(IC)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03435}03435 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (39)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03436}03436 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03437}03437 where \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}\string^\{(IC)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i) \(\backslash\)f\$ and \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)bf V\}\string^\{(IC)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i) \(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03438}03438 are given. The accelerations \(\backslash\)f\$ \(\backslash\)partial\string^2 \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}/\(\backslash\)partial t\string^2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03439}03439 \(\backslash\)f\$ at \(\backslash\)f\$t=t\_0\(\backslash\)f\$ follow from the solution of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03440}03440 (28) and can therefore not be enforced,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03441}03441 unless we wish to initialise the time-\/stepping procedure with a known}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03442}03442 exact solution \(\backslash\)f\$ \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}\string^\{(exact)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i,t) \(\backslash\)f\$. (Only!) in this case}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03443}03443 are we allowed to assign an initial value for the acceleration via}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03444}03444 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03445}03445 \(\backslash\)left. \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i,t)\}\{\(\backslash\)partial t\string^2\} \(\backslash\)right|\_\{t=t\_0\} = }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03446}03446 \{\(\backslash\)bf A\}\string^\{(IC)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i) \(\backslash\)equiv}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03447}03447 \(\backslash\)left. \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 \{\(\backslash\)bf R\}\string^\{(exact)\}(\(\backslash\)xi\string^i,t)\}\{\(\backslash\)partial t\string^2\} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03448}03448 \(\backslash\)right|\_\{t=t\_0\}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03449}03449 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (40)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03450}03450 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03451}03451 We will assume that time-\/stepping is performed with the \(\backslash\)c Newmark }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03452}03452 method which is our default timestepper for hyperbolic}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03453}03453 problems. In this case the time-\/derivatives of the nodal positions in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03454}03454 (28) are replaced by an approximation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03455}03455 which involves the current and three "{}history values"{} of the nodal }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03456}03456 positions. To start the time-\/integration, we need to assign }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03457}03457 suitable values to these quantities to ensure that the intial }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03458}03458 state of the system is represented correctly.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03459}03459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03460}03460 To assign the intial values for the nodal positions, we}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03461}03461 (temporarily) remove all boundary conditions for the nodal }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03462}03462 positions and determine their initial values by solving equation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03463}03463 (38) in its weak form,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03464}03464 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03465}03465 f\_\{il\}\string^\{(0)\} = \(\backslash\)int \(\backslash\)left( \(\backslash\)sum\_\{j=1\}\string^N X\_\{ij\}\string^\{(0)\} \(\backslash\)psi\_j(\(\backslash\)xi\string^k) }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03466}03466 -\/ R\string^\{(IC)\}\_i(\(\backslash\)xi\string^k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03467}03467 \(\backslash\)right) \(\backslash\)psi\_l(\(\backslash\)xi\string^k) \(\backslash\) dv = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03468}03468 \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) for \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$l=1,...,N; \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) i=1,..,3\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03469}03469 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (41)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03470}03470 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03471}03471 where  \(\backslash\)f\$ R\string^\{(IC)\}\_i \(\backslash\)f\$ is the \(\backslash\)f\$i\(\backslash\)f\$-\/th component of }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03472}03472 \(\backslash\)f\$\{\(\backslash\)bf R\}\string^\{(IC)\}.\(\backslash\)f\$ Equation (41) provides}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03473}03473 \(\backslash\)f\$ 3 \(\backslash\)times N\(\backslash\)f\$ equations for the \(\backslash\)f\$ 3 \(\backslash\)times N \(\backslash\)f\$ components}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03474}03474 of the initial nodal positions, \(\backslash\)f\$ X\_\{ij\}\string^\{(0)\} \(\backslash\)f\$ (where}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03475}03475 \(\backslash\)f\$i=1,...3; \(\backslash\) j=1,...,N)\(\backslash\)f\$. To determine the initial nodal}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03477}03477 velocities and solve}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03480}03480 -\/ V\string^\{(IC)\}\_i(\(\backslash\)xi\string^k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03481}03481 \(\backslash\)right) \(\backslash\)psi\_l(\(\backslash\)xi\string^k) \(\backslash\) dv = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03482}03482 \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) for \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$l=1,...,N;  \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) i=1,..,3\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03483}03483 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (42)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03484}03484 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03485}03485 for the initial nodal velocities, \(\backslash\)f\$ X\_\{ij\}\string^\{(1)\} \(\backslash\)f\$ (where}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03492}03492 \(\backslash\)mbox\{ \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) for \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \$l=1,...,N; \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) i=1,..,3\$\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03493}03493 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (43)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03494}03494 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03495}03495 for the initial nodal accelerations, \(\backslash\)f\$ X\_\{ij\}\string^\{(2)\} \(\backslash\)f\$ (where}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03500}03500 \(\backslash\)c Newmark::assign\_initial\_data\_values\_stage2(...) to compute the }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03502}03502 approximations for the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03503}03503 initial velocity and acceleration are correct.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03504}03504 This procedure is fully implemented in the function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03505}03505 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03506}03506 SolidMesh::Solid\_IC\_problem.set\_newmark\_initial\_condition\_directly(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03507}03507 \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03508}03508 whose arguments are:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03509}03509 -\/ The pointer to the problem being solved. This is needed because}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03510}03510   the solution of equations (41) -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03511}03511   (43) requires a temporary change to the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03512}03512   boundary conditions and to the equation numbering scheme. Once}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03513}03513   the history values are assigned, the original}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03514}03514   boundary conditions are restored and the original equation numbers }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03515}03515   are re-\/generated by executing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03516}03516   the Problem's \(\backslash\)c Problem::assign\_eqn\_numbers().}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03517}03517 -\/ A pointer to the \(\backslash\)c SolidMesh on which the initial conditions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03518}03518   are assigned.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03519}03519 -\/ A pointer to the \(\backslash\)c TimeStepper (which has to be of the \(\backslash\)c Newmark}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03520}03520   family).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03521}03521 -\/ A pointer to the "{}Elasic initial condition"{} object (discussed below).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03522}03522 -\/ The initial timestep. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03523}03523 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03524}03524 Here is a brief outline of the implementation:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03525}03525 All \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElements store a pointer to an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03526}03526 \(\backslash\)c SolidInitialCondition object (hierher: change Cond to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03527}03527 Condition in code). By default this pointer is set to NULL,}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03541}03541 // Compute the residuals for the elasticity equations.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03561}03561 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03562}03562 The \(\backslash\)c SolidInitialCondition object stores a (pointer to a) \(\backslash\)c GeomObject}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03563}03563 and a flag that indicates which time-\/derivative (0th, 1st}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03564}03564 or 2nd) of the \(\backslash\)c GeomObject's position vector is to be assigned to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03565}03565 the nodal coordinates. Based on the value of this flag,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03566}03566 the function \(\backslash\)c SolidFiniteElement::get\_residuals\_for\_ic(...),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03567}03567 is able to compute the residuals corresponding to equations}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03568}03568 (41), (42) or }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03569}03569 (43). }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03570}03570 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03571}03571 This all sounds very complicated (and it is!) but luckily}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03572}03572 all the hard work has already been done and the relevant}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03573}03573 procedures are fully implemented. Hence,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03574}03574 the actual assignment of the initial conditions is as simple as}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03575}03575 this:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03576}03576 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03577}03577 \(\backslash\)code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03578}03578 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03579}03579 // Somebody has created a Problem somewhere}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03580}03580 Problem* problem\_pt = new SomeProblem;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03581}03581 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03582}03582 // Somebody has created an SolidMesh somewhere}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03583}03583 SolidMesh* solid\_mesh\_pt = new SomeSolidMesh;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03584}03584 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03585}03585 // Somebody has created a Newmark timestepper somewhere}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03586}03586 TimeStepper* time\_stepper\_pt=new Newmark<1>; }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03587}03587 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03588}03588 [...]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03589}03589 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03590}03590 // Create the GeomObject whose time-\/dependent deformation }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03591}03591 // specifies the initial conditions for our solid body:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03592}03592 // The position vector and its time-\/derivatives}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03593}03593 // are available from GeomObject::dpositiondt(...).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03594}03594 GeomObject* geom\_obj\_pt=new SomeGeomObject;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03595}03595 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03596}03596 //Setup object that specifies the initial conditions:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03597}03597 SolidInitialCondition* ic\_pt = new SolidInitialCondition(geom\_obj\_pt);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03598}03598 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03599}03599 // Choose the initial timestep}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03600}03600 double dt=0.01; }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03601}03601 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03602}03602 // Assign the initial conditions:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03603}03603 SolidMesh::Solid\_IC\_problem.set\_newmark\_initial\_condition\_directly(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03604}03604              problem\_pt,solid\_mesh\_pt,time\_stepper\_pt,IC\_pt,dt);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03605}03605 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03606}03606 // Done!}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03607}03607 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03608}03608 [...]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03609}03609 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03610}03610  \(\backslash\)endcode}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03611}03611 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03612}03612 If we do not know an exact solution to our problem (and in most}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03613}03613 cases we obviously won't...), we can only use the procedure described above}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03614}03614 to determine the initial nodal positions and velocities. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03615}03615 We then need to solve the equations (37) for the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03616}03616 remaining "{}history value"{}. Since the equations (37)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03617}03617 are linear in the accelerations, this is a linear problem}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03618}03618 whose Jacobian matrix is proportional to the mass matrix}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03619}03619 \(\backslash\)f[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03620}03620 M\_\{ij\} = \(\backslash\)int \{\(\backslash\)cal M\} \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)psi\_i \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)psi\_j \(\backslash\) dv. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03621}03621 \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\) (44)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03622}03622 \(\backslash\)f]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03623}03623 The procedure which determines the initial "{}history values"{} }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03624}03624 from the given initial positions and velocities while ensuring}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03625}03625 consistency with the governing equation at \(\backslash\)f\$ t = t\_0\(\backslash\)f\$}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03626}03626 is implemented in }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03627}03627 \(\backslash\)c SolidMesh::Solid\_IC\_problem.set\_newmark\_initial\_condition\_consistently(...)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03628}03628 which takes the same arguments as the function that assigns }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03629}03629 the acceleration directly, but also requires a function pointer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03630}03630 to the "{}multiplier"{} \(\backslash\)f\$  \{\(\backslash\)cal M\} \(\backslash\)f\$.  If there}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03631}03631 is no growth, the multiplier is given by the timescale ratio}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03632}03632 \(\backslash\)f\$\(\backslash\)Lambda\string^2\(\backslash\)f\$; if the body is subjected to uniform isotropic}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03633}03633 growth, \(\backslash\)f\$\(\backslash\)Gamma \(\backslash\)ne 1\(\backslash\)f\$, the multiplier is equal to }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03634}03634 \(\backslash\)f\$\(\backslash\)Gamma \(\backslash\)Lambda\string^2\(\backslash\)f\$. }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03635}03635 If the wrong multiplier is specified (or if it is omitted, in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03636}03636 which the default value of 1.0 is used) the residuals (37)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03637}03637 will be nonzero (or at least larger than the tolerance specified in \(\backslash\)c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03638}03638 SolidICProblem). In this case a warning is issued and the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03639}03639 code execution terminates. This behaviour can be suppressed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03640}03640 by increasing the tolerance suitably, but you do this at your own risk!}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03641}03641 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03642}03642 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03643}03643 <B>Important:</B> }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03644}03644 The above procedures can only handle the assignment of }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03645}03645 initial conditions in problems that are formulated in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03646}03646 terms of displacements and do \(\backslash\)b not involve any additional variables}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03647}03647 such as solid pressures. We do not believe that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03648}03648 it is possible to implement the assignment of initial conditions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03649}03649 for such problems without additional knowledge about the precise }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03650}03650 form of the constitutive equations. If the presence of "{}internal}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03651}03651 solid Data"{} is detected during the assignment of the initial}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03652}03652 guess, code execution terminates with an appropriate warning message.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03653}03653 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{leftovers_8txt__doxygenified_8h_source_l03654}03654 }
